optional premises are to be used in this regard there is no limitation on the number of days which a licensee may specify in each notice part 1994   severability if any part section subsection sentence clause or phrase of this chapter is for any reason held to be invalid such decision shall not affect the validity of the remaining portions of this chapter  and the city council declares it would have passed the ordinance codified in this chapter and each part section subsection sentence clause or phrase thereof regardless of the fact that any one or more parts sections subsections sentences clauses or phrases be declared invalid part 1994 sexually oriented businesses purpose and intent the purpose and intent of this chapter is to regulate sexually oriented businesses to promote the health safety and general welfare of the citizens of the city and to establish reasonable and uniform regulations to prevent the deleterious location and design of sexually oriented businesses within the city thereby reducing or eliminating the adverse secondary effects from such sexually oriented businesses the provisions of this chapter are not intended to impose a limitation or restriction on the content of any communicative materials including sexually oriented materials it is not the intent of this chapter to restrict or deny access by adults to sexually oriented materials protected by the first amendment or the colorado constitution or to deny access by the distributors and exhibitors of sexually oriented entertainment to their intended market neither is it the intent nor effect of this chapter to condone or legitimize the distribution of obscene material  part 2001   definitions a words and phrases used in this chapter shall have the following meanings ascribed to them adult arcade means any commercial establishment to which the public is permitted or invited where for any form of consideration one or more still or motion picture projectors slide projectors or similar machines or other image or virtual reality producing machines for viewing by five or fewer persons per machine at any one time are used regularly to show films motion pictures video cassettes slides or other photographic digital or electronic reproductions describing simulating or depicting specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas adult bookstore adult novelty store or adult video means a commercial establishment that as one of its principal business purposes offers for sale or rental for any form of consideration any one or more of the following 1 books magazines periodicals or other printed matter or photographs films motion pictures video cassettes or video reproductions slides or other visual representations however produced that depict or describe specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas  or 2 instruments devices or paraphernalia which are designed for use in connection with specified sexual activities adult cabaret means a nightclub bar restaurant concert hall auditorium or other commercial establishment that features 1 persons who appear nude or in a state of nudity or seminudity  or 2 live performances that are characterized by the exposure of specified anatomical areas or by the exhibition of specified sexual activities adult motel means a hotel motel or similar commercial establishment that offers accommodations to the public for any form of consideration and provides patrons with closedcircuit television transmission films motion pictures video cassettes slides or other media productions however produced which are characterized by the depiction or description of specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas and which commercial establishment has a sign visible from the public rightofway which advertises the availability of this adult type of media production adult motion picture theater means a commercial establishment that is distinguished or characterized by the showing for any form of consideration of films motion pictures video cassettes slides or similar photographic reproductions on more than one hundred 100 days per year that have an x rating or that have an emphasis on depicting or describing specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas adult theater means a theater concert hall auditorium or similar commercial establishment that for any form of consideration regularly features persons who appear in a state of nudity or live performances which are characterized by an emphasis on exposure of specified anatomical areas or by specified sexual activities commercial establishment may have other principal business purposes that do not involve the depicting or describing specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas and still be categorized as a sexually oriented business such other business purposes will not serve to exempt such commercial establishments from being categorized as a sexually oriented business so long as one of its principal business purposes is the offering for sale or rental for consideration the specified materials that depict or describe specified sexual activities or specified anatomical areas the term commercial establishment includes clubs fraternal organizations social organizations civic organizations or other similar organizations with paid memberships employee means a person who works or performs in andor for a sexually oriented business regardless of whether or not said person is paid a salary wage or other compensation by the operator of said business establishment of a sexually oriented business means and includes any of the following 1 the opening or commencement of any such business as a new business  2 the conversion of an existing business into a sexually oriented business  3 the addition of a different sexually oriented business to any other existing sexually oriented business  4 the relocation of a sexually oriented business foyer means an architectural element of a building that consists of an entry hall or vestibule that is completely enclosed and contains one door to provide access to areas outside of the building and a separate door to provide access to areas inside of the building licensee means a person in whose name a license to operate a sexually oriented business has been issued as well as the individual listed as an applicant on the application for a sexually oriented business license licenses available to licensees are type a and type b licenses as more particularly described in of this licensing officer means the city clerk or his or her designee manager means an operator other than a licensee who is employed by a sexually oriented business to act as a manager or supervisor of employees or is otherwise responsible for the operation of the business nudity or state of nudity means 1 the appearance of human bare buttock anus male genitals female genitals or the areola or nipple of the female breast  or 2 a state of dress which fails opaquely and fully to cover human buttocks anus male or female genitals pubic region or areola or nipple of the female breast nude model studio means any place where a person who appears in a state of nudity or displays specified anatomical areas is provided for money or any form of consideration to be observed sketched drawn painted sculpted photographed or similarly depicted by other persons operator means and includes the owner license holder custodian manager operator or person in charge of any licensed premises peep booth means a room semienclosure or other similar area located within a licensed premises wherein a person may view representations of specified anatomical areas or specified sexual activities person means an individual proprietorship partnership corporation limited liability company association or other legal entity premises or licensed premises means any premises that requires a sexually oriented business license and that is classified as a sexually oriented business including parking lots and sidewalks immediately adjacent to the structure containing the sexually oriented business principal business purpose means as to any establishment having as a substantial or significant portion of its stock in trade the items listed in subparagraphs 1 and 2 of the definition of adult bookstore adult novelty store or adult video store above and having on the premises at least thirty percent of the establishments display space occupied by the display of the items described therein principal owner means any person owning directly or beneficially 1 ten 10 percent or more of the membership interests in a limited liability company  2 in the case of any other legal entity ten 10 percent or more of the ownership interests in the entity public park means an area of land owned by a governmental entity and intended to be used for recreational purposes but not including any such land that contains no improvements and is intended only for open space purposes and not including any such land that is intended for use only for pathway purposes sexually oriented business means an adult arcade adult bookstore adult novelty shop adult video store adult cabaret adult motel adult motion picture theater adult theater or nude model studio the definition of sexually oriented business shall not include an establishment where a medical practitioner psychologist psychiatrist or similar professional person licensed by the state of colorado engages in medically approved and recognized sexual therapy seminude or seminudity means a state of dress in which clothing covers no more than the genitals pubic region and areola of the female breasts as well as portions of the body covered by supporting straps or devices which supporting straps or devices are used to support or enable the wearing of such clothing specified anatomical areas as used in this definition means and includes any of the following 1 human genitals pubic region buttocks anus or female breasts below a point immediately above the top of the areola that are not completely and opaquely covered  2 human male genitals in a discernibly turgid state even if completely and opaquely covered specified criminal acts means sexual crimes against children sexual abuse sexual assault or crimes connected with another sexually oriented business including but not limited to distribution of obscenity prostitution or pandering specified sexual activities means and includes any of the following 1 the fondling or other intentional touching of human genitals pubic region buttocks anus or female breasts  2 sex acts normal or perverted actual or simulated including intercourse oral copulation or sodomy  3 masturbation actual or simulated  4 human genitals in a state of sexual stimulation arousal or tumescence  5 excretory functions as part of or in connection with any of the activities set forth in subsections 1 of this definition transfer of ownership or control of a sexually oriented business means and includes any of the following 1 the sale lease or sublease of the business  2 the transfer of securities that constitute a controlling interest in the business whether by sale exchange or similar means  or 3 the establishment of a trust management arrangement gift or other similar legal device that transfers ownership or control of the business including a transfer by bequest or operation of law b the definitions set forth in subsection a of this section shall apply with respect to the use of the same terms elsewhere in this code including but not limited to title 17 unless a different definition is specifically contained in such other chapter or title in this code  part 2001   interior lighting regulations a the interior portion of the premises of a sexually oriented business to which patrons are permitted access shall be equipped with overhead lighting fixtures of sufficient intensity to illuminate every place including peep booths at an illumination of not less than five 5 foot candles as measured at the floor level b it shall be the duty of the licensee and employees present on the more fully described in chapters 1748 and 1752 of this the location requirements set forth in paragraph c of this section shall apply as a further limitation in all zone districts where sexually oriented businesses are permitted pursuant to paragraph a of this section c it shall be unlawful to operate or cause to be operated a sexually oriented business within five hundred 500 feet of 1 any religious institution as that term is defined in   2 any school meeting all requirements of the compulsory education laws of the state of colorado  3 any residential zone district whether or not developed established and identified in chapters 1716 1720 1724 and 1728  4 any existing dwelling unit whether singlefamily or multifamily as those terms are defined in that is occupied by its owner or by persons authorized by the owner to occupy such dwelling unit or has been vacant for less than six 6 months  5 any child care center as that term is defined in   6 any public park as described in this   7 any recreational and social facility as those terms are defined in which is regularly open to and used by children under the age of eighteen 18 years d it shall be unlawful to cause or permit the operation establishment or maintenance of a sexually oriented business within one hundred 100 feet of any other sexually oriented business e all exterior windows in a sexually oriented business shall be opaque to such an extent that interior objects viewed from outside shall be so obscure as to be unidentifiable exterior windows in sexually oriented businesses shall not be used for any display or sign except for a sign that complies with the requirements of f all doors for ingress and egress to a sexually oriented business except emergency exits used only for emergency purposes shall be located on the front of the sexually oriented business for purposes of this subsection the front of a sexually oriented business shall be deemed to be that facade of the building that faces the front lot line of the lot or parcel on which the business is located every sexually oriented business shall have a foyer at every point of ingress or egress except for emergency exits part 2001   measurement of distance a the distance between any two 2 sexually oriented businesses shall be measured in a straight line without regard to intervening structures from the closest point on the property line of a parcel upon which a sexually oriented business operates to the closest point on the property line of a parcel upon which the proposed sexually oriented business is proposed to operate b the distance between any sexually oriented business and any religious institution school dwelling unit child care center public park recreational or social facility shall be measured in a straight line without regard to intervening structures or objects from the closest point on the property line of the parcel upon which a sexually oriented business operates to the closest point on the property line of the premises of a religious institution school dwelling unit child care center public park or recreational and social facility c the distance between any sexually oriented business and any residential or other zone district where sexually oriented businesses are prohibited shall be measured in a straight line without regard to intervening structures or objects from the closest point on the property line of the sexually oriented business to the closest point on the property line of the residential or other zone district where sexually oriented businesses are prohibited  part 2001   other locational regulations a a sexually oriented business which at the time it received its sexually oriented business license was in compliance with the location requirements of not violate that section if when the sexually oriented business applies to renew its valid sexually oriented business license pursuant to the provisions of a religious institution school dwelling unit child care center public park or recreational and social facility is then located within five hundred 500 feet of the sexually oriented business or if by virtue of a zone change or the annexation and zoning of new territory not previously in the city a residential or other zone district where sexually oriented businesses are prohibited is then located within five hundred 500 feet of the sexually oriented business this provision applies only to the renewal of a valid sexually oriented business license and does not apply to an application for a sexually oriented business license that is submitted as a result of the previous sexually oriented business license at the same location expiring or being revoked  part 2001   stage required in adult cabaret and adult theater any adult cabaret or adult theater shall have one or more separate areas designated as a stage in the diagram submitted as part of the application for the sexually oriented business license entertainers shall perform only upon a stage the stage shall be fixed and immovable and located inside the building in which the adult use operates no seating for the audience shall be permitted within three feet of the edge of the stage no members of the audience shall be permitted upon the stage or within three 3 feet of the edge of the stage  part 2001   conduct in sexually oriented business a no licensee manager or employee mingling with the patrons of a sexually oriented business or serving food or drinks shall be in a state of nudity it is a defense to any prosecution for a violation of this subsection that an employee of a sexually oriented business exposed any specified anatomical area only during the employees bona fide use of a restroom or during the employees bona fide use of a dressing room that is accessible only to employees b no licensee manager or employee shall encourage or knowingly permit any person upon the premises to touch caress or fondle the genitals pubic region buttocks anus or breasts of any person  part 2001   employee tips a it shall be unlawful for any employee of a sexually oriented business to receive tips from patrons except as set forth in subsection c of this section b a licensee that desires to provide for tips from its patrons shall establish one or more boxes or other containers to receive tips all tips for such employees shall be placed by the patron of the sexually oriented business into the tip box c a sexually oriented business that provides tip boxes for its patrons as provided in this section shall post one or more signs to be conspicuously visible to the patrons on the premises in bold letters at least one inch high to read as follows all tips are to be placed in the tip box and not handed directly to employees any physical contact between a patron and employees is strictly prohibited  part 2001   unlawful acts and penalties a it shall be unlawful for an operator licensee manager or employee to violate any of the requirements of this chapter or establishment if the city manager determines that a cause for suspension or revocation exists he or she shall issue an order suspending or revoking the sexually oriented business license within thirty 197 as amended  1981   purpose the purpose of the ordinance codified in this chapter is to declare what is a nuisance within the city limits and to provide remedies for the abatement of the same  1981   nuisance defined nuisance means any act or condition which either a injuriously affects the safety health or morals of the public  or b obstructs the free use of property so as to interfere with the comfortable enjoyment of life or property  or c works some substantial annoyance inconvenience or injury to the public  part 1981   nuisances prohibited no person being the owner agent or occupant of or having under his control any building lot or premises shall maintain or allow any nuisance to be or remain thereon nor shall any person permit or cause any nuisance to exist within the city limits  1981   nuisances designated a nuisance may include but is not limited to the acts or conditions specifically declared to be nuisances in this chapter  provided that the same act or condition either a injuriously affects the safety health or morals of the public  or b obstructs the free use of property so as to interfere with the comfortable enjoyment of life or property  or c works some substantial annoyance inconvenience or injury to the public l  l0 part 1981   stagnant ponds any cellar vault drain sewer pond of water or other place upon or within any private premises or grounds in this city that is nauseous or offensive to others or injurious to public health accumulation or deposition of nauseous offensive or foul water or other substances is a nuisance and may be abated as provided in this chapter a 1981   open wells cisterns or excavations excavations exceeding five 5 feet in depth cisterns and wells or an excavation used for storage of water are public nuisances unless the same are adequately covered with a locked lid or other covering weighing at least sixty 60 pounds or are securely fenced with a solid fence to a height of at least five 5 feet and may be abated as provided in this chapter b 1981   unauthorized handbills posters and placards any handbill poster placard or painted or printed matter which is stuck posted or pasted upon any public or private house store or other buildings or upon any fence power pole telephone pole or other structure without the permission of the owner agent or occupant of the house is a nuisance c 1981   flyproducing conditions the following are nuisances a any accumulation of manure on premises where animals are kept unless the premises are kept clean and the manure is kept in a box or vault which is screened from flies and emptied at least once each week  b privies vaults cesspools pits or like places which are not securely screened to protect them from flies  c trash litter rags or anything whatsoever in which flies may breed or multiply  or d garbage in any quantity which is not covered or screened to protect it from flies d 1981   junkyards and dumping grounds all places used or maintained as junkyards or dumping grounds or for the wrecking or disassembling of automobiles trucks tractors or machinery of any kind or for the storing or leaving of worn out wrecked or abandoned automobiles trucks tractors trailers boats and housetrailers or machinery of any kind or of any of the parts thereof or for the storing or leaving of any machinery or equipment used by contractors or builders or by other persons which places are kept in such manner as to essentially interfere with the comfortable enjoyment of life or property by others are a nuisance and may be abated as provided in this chapter e 1981   contaminated or impure wells any well or cistern on any property within the city whenever a chemical analysis or other proper test shows that the water of the well or cistern is contaminated impure or unwholesome is a nuisance f 1981   defective drains ditches tanks or garbage cans any unclean leaking foul unsafe or dangerous defective or filthy drain ditch tank or gutter or stinking fat grease or other matter it is unlawful to keep collect or use or cause to be kept collected or used in this city any stale putrid or stinking fat or grease or other matter such conditions are a nuisance and may be abated as provided in this chapter j 1981   throwing rubbish into sewer it is unlawful to throw or deposit or cause or permit to be thrown and deposited in any purpose of this section a nuisance per se is expressly defined as a nuisance which is a nuisance at all times and under all circumstances regardless of location or surroundings a nuisance which is not a nuisance per se shall be abated following a judicial determination by the municipal court that a nuisance exists however in all cases the city may summarily abate any nuisance in or upon any street avenue alley sidewalk highway or other public property within the city  1981   abatement expense assessment and lien any expense incurred by the city in the abatement of a nuisance in accordance with lumber leaves straw or other like combustible material in any street alley or vacant lot except by special permission of the chief of the fire department when such burning shall be done in screened metal receptacles approved by him and under such proper safeguards as he may direct as to time and weather  provided that the chief of the fire department may issue a general permit by publication during certain seasons of the year for the burning of leaves or other like material where conducted during daylight and with an adult in constant attendance  b any person or persons to dispose of place or dump empty boxes barrels leaves trash wastepaper excelsior or other like combustible materials in any alley or on any sidewalk or vacant lot or premises within thirty 30 feet of any building except by special permission of the chief of the fire department  c any person or persons to place ashes within any building in any box barrel or other wooden vessel or upon any wooden vessel or floor  d any person or persons to keep on any premises any oily waste or oily rags unless at all times when not actually in use such oily waste and oily rags are kept in a ventilated metal can with selfclosing cover and riveted joints standing on metal legs which raise the bottom of the container at least five 5 inches above the floor  e any person or persons to keep or deposit any ashes or combustible refuse unless same is kept or deposited in a safe secure incombustible container with adequate openings at top and bottom  and every owner or occupant of property where ashes are kept or deposited shall erect and maintain upon the premises a permanently affixed incombustible ash pit for that purpose so located as not to endanger walls fences or other combustible material when located in a yard such ash pits shall be so placed as to create no nuisance to adjoining property and in no case shall they be located within a shed or at such location as to create a fire hazard the primary duty of erecting such ash pits shall be upon the owner of such premises but in the event that such owner fails neglects or refuses to erect such ash pits such failure neglect or refusal shall in no way excuse the occupant of such premises from the erection of the same ash pits shall be cleaned at least once each week and at such shorter intervals as may be necessary  f any person or persons to pile or store hay straw lumber or other combustible material unless the same are completely enclosed within buildings  provided that the chief of the fire department may by special permission authorize such storage when in his opinion the same does not constitute a fire hazard  g any person or persons to store or keep any dynamite nitroglycerin giant powder bulk can powder or other explosives in any building storeroom or warehouse within the city limits except as hereafter provided any person or persons desiring to store or keep any such dynamite nitroglycerin giant powder gun powder or other explosives shall make written application to the chief of the fire department for permission to do so which application shall describe the amount of such explosives desired to be kept or stored by such applicant and the facilities and place such applicant proposes for the storage of the same if in the opinion of the chief of the fire department the facilities for storage are safe considering the type and quantity of explosives desired to be stored then the chief of the fire department may issue a permit for such storage  provided that such explosives shall at all times be kept in magazines made of fireproof material and kept securely locked except when necessarily opened for use by authorized persons and further provided that such magazines shall be conspicuously labelled in red letters at least four 4 inches high explosives and located within the building on the ground floor within ten 10 feet of a street entrance  1938   sale use and possession of fireworks a adjacent to any street sidewalk or alleyway in which the undesirable growth is found which abatement notice shall advise such person of the existence of the undesirable growth the notice shall be in writing shall state that undesirable growth exists and constitutes a hazard or nuisance shall inform the addressee that he or she must within five 5 days after service or receipt of such notice cause the undesirable growth to be removed and the property cleaned or the accumulation otherwise remedied  and shall advise the addressee of the possible penalties for noncompliance with this chapter such notice shall be served by mailing a copy of the notice to the address of the occupant and to the address of the owner or agent of the property as set forth in the records of the county assessor of fremont county colorado proper notice shall be deemed to have been given when properly addressed and deposited in the united states mail with the proper amount of postage attached such notice shall be deemed to have been received three 3 days after proper mailing if there is more than one 1 owner of the premises or more than one 1 occupant of the premises who is not an owner notice as provided for prohibited legislative declaration the city council of the city of florence finds and declares that noise is a major source of environmental pollution which represents a threat to the serenity and quality of life in the city of florence excess noise often has an adverse physiological and psychological effect on human beings thus contributing to an economic loss to the community accordingly it is the policy of the city to establish standards for noise level limits for various time periods and areas within the city limits of the city of florence as well as within all areas over which the city of florence has jurisdiction noise in excess of the limits provided in this chapter constitutes a public nuisance part 2006   definitions as used in this chapter unless the context otherwise requires commercial zone means a general commercial district central historic district or business professional district as those districts are represented on the most recent zoning district map of the city of florence dba means sound levels in decibels measured on the a scale of a standard sound level meter having characteristics defined by the american national standards institute publication s141971 decibel means a unit used to express the magnitude of a change in sound level the difference in decibels between two 2 sound pressure levels is twenty 20 times the common logarithm of their ratio in sound pressure measurements sound levels are defined as twenty 20 times the common logarithm of the ratio of that sound pressure level to a reference level of 2  105 nm 2 newtonsmeter squared as an example of the effect of the formula a three 3 decibel change is a one hundred 100 percent increase or decrease in the sound level and a ten 10 decibel change is a one thousand 1000 percent increase or decrease in the sound level industrial zone means a light industrial district i1 or heavy industrial district i2 as those districts are represented on the most recent zoning district map of the city of florence motor vehicle motordriven cycle offhighway vehicle and vehicle mean the same as those definitions found at crs 421102 1973 as amended or any future codification person means any natural person firm partnership association corporation or company residential zone means a residential estates district r1 low density residential district r2 low medium density residential district r3 high density residential district manufactured home district manufactured home park district recreational vehicle park district or planned unit development pud as those districts and puds are represented on the most recent zoning district map of the city of florence part 2006   noise prohibited it is unlawful for any person to make or cause to be made any continuous impulsive or periodic noise which a is of such unusual or exceptional character intensity or duration that it disturbs injures or endangers the comfort repose health peace or safety of any person or causes damage to any property  or b exceeds the levels set forth in part 2006   maximum permissible noise levels a every activity to which this section is applicable shall be conducted in a manner so that any noise produced is not objectionable due to intermittence beat frequency or shrillness sound levels of noise radiating from a property line at a distance of twentyfive 25 feet or more therefrom in excess of the dba established for the following time periods and zones shall constitute prima facie evidence that such noise is a public nuisance and an infraction hereunder zone  am to next  pm  pm to next  am residential 55 dba 50 dba commercial 60 dba 55 dba light industrial 70 dba 65 dba heavy industrial 80 dba 75 dba b in the hours between seven  am and the next seven  pm the noise levels permitted in subsection a of this section for light industrial and heavy industrial zones may be increased by ten 10 dba for a period not to exceed fifteen 15 minutes in any one 1 hour period c periodic impulsive or shrill noises shall be considered a public nuisance and an infraction hereunder when such noises are at a sound level of five 5 dba less than those listed in subsection a of this section d in all sound measurements consideration shall be given to the effect of the ambient noise level created by the encompassing noise of the environment from all sources at the time and place of such sound level measurement part 2006   exceptions the maximum dba specified in not apply to sound from a any bell or chime from any building clock school or church  b any siren whistle or bell lawfully used by peddler means any person who travels within the city of florence conveying or transporting goods wares or merchandise or offering or exposing the same for sale or making sales and delivering articles to purchasers b solicitor means any person who travels within the city of florence soliciting or taking or attempting to take orders for sale or purchase of goods wares or merchandise including magazines books periodicals real or personal property of any nature whatsoever for future delivery or for services to be performed or for the donation of money or financial assistance whether or not such individual has carries or exposes for sale a sample of the subject of such order or whether or not he is collecting advance payment on such orders such definition includes any person who for himself or for another person firm or corporation hires leases uses or occupies any building motor vehicle trailer structure tent railroad boxcar hotel or motel room lodging house apartment shop or any streets alleys or other place within the city for the primary purpose of exhibiting samples and taking orders for future delivery c itinerant merchant or transient merchant means any individual corporation business trust estate trust partnership limited liability company association joint venture or any other commercial entity that on a temporary basis sells leases takes orders or delivers goods wares food merchandise or other tangible personal property in the city by a retail sale  or makes such sale from a temporary location which includes any location other than a building as defined at d pushcart vendor means a vendor who would otherwise be considered an itinerant merchant but who vends goods wares food or other merchandise on a retail basis from a pushcart that is capable of being moved by hand from one location to another part 1996  2 1212008   license requiredapplication a it shall be unlawful for any peddler solicitor or transient merchant to engage in any such enforcement the florence police department shall enforce the provisions of this chapter part 1996   penalty any person group corporation partnership or other legal entity who violates any provision of definitions as used in this chapter a loitering means remaining idle in essentially one location and shall include the concept of spending time idly being dilatory lingering staying sauntering delaying and standing around and shall also include the colloquial expressions hanging around and hanging out the term shall also include such activity by the driver or a passenger in a motor vehicle which is parked standing or being driven on any public street alley or parking lot b public place means any street alley highway sidewalk park playground or place to which the general public has access and a right to resort for business entertainment or other lawful purpose a public place shall include but not be limited to any store shop restaurant tavern bowling alley cafe theater drug store pool room shopping center and any other place devoted to the amusement or entertainment of the general public it shall also include the front or immediate area of the above c going to or returning from means travel directly to or from any activity excepted from the coverage of this chapter which travel shall not exceed a period of thirty 30 minutes prior to the commencement of such activity or subsequent to the termination of such activity part 1996   juvenile loitering during nighttime hours prohibited a it shall be unlawful for any person under the age of eighteen 18 years to loiter or to aimlessly drive or ride about on or about any street avenue highway road sidewalk curb gutter parking lot alley vacant lot park cemetery playground yard building place of amusement or eating place whether public or private or any other public place during the hours beginning at  am on saturday and sunday mornings and ending at six  am  and beginning at ten  pm on sunday night night and ending at six  am the following mornings no violation of this section will have occurred if the person under the age of eighteen 18 years is accompanied by a parent guardian or other adult over the age of twentyone 21 years who is authorized in writing by a parent or guardian of such juvenile to take said parents place in accompanying said juvenile for a designated period of time and purpose within a specified area b this section shall not apply and no person shall be charged with a violation of this section or arrested therefor if such person was 1 not loitering  or 2 in a parked standing or moving motor vehicle while accompanied by a parent guardian or other adult person over the age of twentyone 21 years who is authorized in writing by a parent or guardian of a person under the age of eighteen 18 years to take the parents or guardians place in accompanying the juvenile for a designated period of time and purpose within a specified area  or 3 in a motor vehicle in interstate travel  or 4 engaged in any lawful employment or participating in any school religious or athletic activity or going to or returning from any such activity or going to or from any other activities of any kind which are supervised or directed by adult persons over the age of twentyone 21 years  provided that such adult persons have the authority of the parents of the persons under the age of eighteen 18 years who are participating in or attending such event or activity to conduct and to supervise the event or activity  and further provided that the group or organization has given the police department not less than seventytwo 72 hours advance written notice of the event or activity  or 5 married or an otherwise emancipated minor part 1996   parental responsibility it shall be unlawful for the parent guardian or other adult having the care and custody of a juvenile under the age of eighteen 18 years to knowingly permit or allow such juvenile to loiter or to aimlessly drive or ride about at the places and within the times prohibited by this chapter the term knowingly includes knowledge which a parent guardian or other adult person having responsibility for a juvenile should be reasonably expected to have concerning the whereabouts of a juvenile in that parents guardians or other adult persons custody it shall be no defense that a parent guardian or other adult person having the care and custody of the juvenile was indifferent to the activities conduct or whereabouts of such juvenile part 1996   business owner or operator responsibility it shall be a violation of this for any proprietor owner or operator of any public place or any agent or employee of such proprietor owner or operator to permit a juvenile to remain in his establishment during the hours prohibited by this chapter unless the minor is accompanied by a parent guardian or other adult person over the age of twentyone 21 years which adult has the written authority of a parent or guardian of the juvenile to have control of the juvenile or unless necessary for medical purposes or for an activity which is excepted from the applicability of the curfew by the terms of this chapter whenever a juvenile continues to remain at such an establishment after the proprietor owner operator or other person in charge orders him to leave the proprietor owner operator or other person in charge shall immediately notify the police department of the violation part 1996   penalties any person who violates any of the provisions of this may be found guilty of a civil infraction and shall be subject to a fine of not less than fifty dollars $5000 nor more than one thousand dollars $100000 the minimum fine provided under this section shall not be suspended by the municipal court part 1996   severability if any provision of this chapter or the application thereof to any person or circumstances is held invalid such invalidity shall not affect other provisions or applications of this chapter which can be given effect without the invalid provision or application and to this end the provisions of this chapter are declared to be severable part 1996 title 10  vehicles and traffic time idly  to be dilatory  to linger  to stay  to saunter  to delay  to stand around  and shall also include the colloquial expression hanging around or hanging out part 2002   pedestrian may correct the condition and the permittee shall be responsible for repaving and repair costs occasioned thereby furthermore the permittee shall discontinue any and all other excavation work within the public rightsofway within the city and shall be issued no additional excavation permits until such time as the required repair has been completed and paid for by permittee  2003   excavation listed in this section those standards shall be known as the florence street standards the city manager is given the authority to make interpretations and minor modifications to the florence street standards for any conflicting or unclear items in the event portions of the florence street standards conflict with the florence subdivision regulations or adopted building codes the building codes and subdivision regulations shall prevail and supercede any such conflicting provision in the florence street standards the fremont sanitation district will remain responsible for all elements of the sanitary sewer facility design construction and maintenance within the city of florence in the event portions of the florence street standards conflict with the sanitary sewer design standards currently used by the fremont sanitation district the requirements of the fremont sanitation district shall prevail and supercede any such conflicting provision in the florence street standards the florence minimum street design standards presented in table 1 of appendix a of the florence subdivision regulations shall prevail as minimum standard for the design parameters listed in that table line to the point of use regardless of the meter setting service main means a water line six 6 inches or smaller that services one 1 or more service lines or taps which does not loop back to transmission or branch lines does not carry fire flow nor does it extend beyond twelve hundred 1200 lineal feet if extension beyond twelve hundred 1200 lineal feet is required or future development is anticipated sizing shall be as a branch main line shall  may whenever shall is used herein it shall be construed as a mandatory direction  whenever may is used herein it shall be construed as a permissive but not mandatory direction stop and waste valve means plumbing valve at the customers end of the service line for the customers use prior to any customer branch piping or water use superintendent means that person appointed by the city manager to supervise the operation and maintenance of the city water facilities tap or water connection means the connecting of the service line from the structure which it is to serve to the public water system either directly to a public main line or indirectly private main line tracer wire mans a metallic wire installed for the length of a plastic pipe for the purpose of making such pipe capable of detection transmission main line means a conduit to provide water for branching and service water mains which is six 6 inches or larger capable of conveying fire flow branch and service main water demands travel charge means a charge assessed for travel to customers for whom the city provides services at the request of the customer other than normal installation and maintenance of city equipment property and lines it also includes travel required for customers who fail to comply with the citys requirements thereby causing the city to do the work necessary for customers compliance when required the travel charge shall be in addition to the actual costs of the work done wholesale water use means a person or entity that purchases treated water for resale to other consumers any other term any other term not herein defined shall be defined as presented in the glossary water and sewage control engineering apha awwa asce and fwsa latest editions a copy of which is available for inspection lpart 1990   application for water service a anyone requesting water service shall be required to complete an agreement for water service an application and pay all fees required before action will be taken by the city manager on a request for water service if the applicant is dissatisfied with action taken by the city manager he may request that the city council review said action the council shall have the right to review and revise the action taken by the city manager there shall be no appeal from the action taken by the city council if the application is accepted the applicant shall agree and shall be deemed to have consented to comply with all ordinances and regulations in effect as well as those subsequently adopted b application for service does not bind the applicant to use the service such applications shall be retained along with fees paid by the city for a period of three hundred sixtyfive 365 days if the applicant has not then requested a service connection the application shall be deemed to be withdrawn the city may retain the fees paid until a refund is requested in writing however debt retirement fees from the date of application and a handling charge of ten percent 10% of application fee shall be retained a new application shall then be required any refunds shall be made without interest part 1990   rescission of approval the council reserves the right to rescind any approval previously granted for water service before service has been provided lpart 1990   denial of application the city reserves the exclusive right to deny any water service application for any reason which may include but are not limited to the following a the service applied for would create an excessive seasonal or other demand on the facilities  b there exists an unresolved obligation between the city and the applicant  c there is not provided adequate documentation of easements for water lines serving the property  d connection of the water system to applicants existing plumbing would constitute a crossconnection to an unsafe water supply  e there is a material misrepresentation in the application as to the property or fixtures contained in the property  f there has been a misrepresentation concerning use to be made of water  g in the judgment of the city council service to the property is not reasonably feasible based on engineering and economic considerations part 1990   water meter replacement and service line responsibility a all owners users andor occupants of property or premises served with municipal water shall keep and repair all service lines upon their premises and property up to the border of any adjoining curb or street in place including stopcocks and connecting lines at their own expense regardless of the location of the municipal water meter b if a service line or associated devices on the customers property are found to be defective or damaged the city manager shall require the owner to upgrade or pay for the city to upgrade such service line to include items such as accurate metering devices proper metering location proper fittings and meter pit or proper service line sizing under the following guidelines 1 following a meter test  owner or city requested the city will bear fifty percent 50% of the total cost to upgrade the metering set which could include water meter meter setter meter pit meter pit cover associated valves piping and related labor costs the intent of this section is to assist water users with nonuniform meter settings to upgrade to uniform standards the city will diligently minimize such costs for both parties and maintain a uniform standard 2 the owner may make arrangements to pay their fifty percent 50% share of the total cost over twelve 12 equal continuous monthly payments for a ten percent 10% accounting charge added to the owners share 3 service lines are defined as any pipe line or conduit including curbstop used to provide water service from the main line to a building or dwelling unit the city shall have no monetary liability whatsoever in respect thereto from the customers property line to the point of use regardless of the meter setting and such water charges for water metered by a defective or leaking service line are the sole responsibility of the owner at all times however the city has sole responsibility for that portion of the service line from the water main tap to the edge of the customers property line 4 changes in customers equipment or service  or conditions affecting the meter pit  are the sole responsibility of the owner c 1 after a new water tap has been performed and meets a uniform standard or a meter setting has been upgraded to such a standard the owner has full and complete responsibility to pay for costs to maintain such meter setting to such uniform standards set by the city council including the responsibility to maintain the water meter to the standard as set by the meter test the city will on the owners behalf act as the owners agent to the manufacturer of the water meters and equipment to seek manufacturer warranty repair or replacement of that equipment installed to minimize such cost to the owner 2 the city will at all times supply all related equipment and material for connection to the municipal water system to maintain a uniform standard except the customers service line from the meter setting to the customers point of use    commercial and industrial users industrial or commercial users within or without the city may make application for a contract with the city in which rates terms and conditions of use and manner of payment shall be specified nothing herein shall require the city to enter into such a contract lpart 1990   water line extensionsconditions no water main pipe or water meter and related fitting shall be extended constructed installed or attached to the city water system unless the same are extended under a public street or other public rightofway or utility easement dedicated or otherwise created for the benefit of the public or under private premises to which the city shall by private easement rightofway or permission have the right to install and maintain such water line or lines part 1990   water main line extensionssubmission of plans a city water mains and service lines shall not be extended unless the applicant for the water service pays in advance to the city the complete cost of installation in addition to such charges and tap fees the applicant for water service may be required to provide a water main line or lines as determined by the city manager based upon projected usage and city looping requirements at a minimum transmission or branch water mains shall not be less than six 6 inches in diameter shall contain at least one 1 valve to isolate the main extension from the water system and shall have at least one 1 fire hydrant at the end of the extension for flushing and fire protection additional valves hydrants and increased pipe diameters may be required depending on the length of such main line extensions if a service main is allowed it shall include an isolation valve from the branch main and a means of flushing b all owners subdividers contractors and builders shall submit to the city manager detailed plans for any proposed utility installations which shall include capacities sizes location of mains fittings fire hydrants tanks pumps and pump houses and the location of loopings and grids to existing city mains the materials for installation and the labor costs for installation of all required items shall be at the sole expense of the owner subdivider contractor or builder the capacity size and material of all required items to be installed their locations and the manner and specification for their installation shall be determined by the city manager part 1990   water service linesextensions pressure required installation requirements a existing water service lines shall not be extended or added onto unless written permission is obtained from the city manager a water service line shall not extend more than two hundred fifty 250 feet beyond the main line physical tap connection unless pipe sizing or other provisions a residual pressure at the customers point of use is at least twentyfive 25 pounds per square inch gauge psig when eighty percent 80% of the metering devices rated flow in the service line is present b plastic service lines may be used if a tracer wire is provided to locate such a service line in the future c all service lines shall have a shutoff valve accessible at the point of use before any branch piping to provide a means for maintenance and emergency shutoff a travel charge as set forth herein shall be levied if the city is required to utilize city valves for such a purpose part 1990   water main rebate agreements for line extensions within the corporate limits of the city a the city council may from time to time enter into contracts with persons whereby a portion of the cost of the installation of an eight 8 inch or larger water main extension or enlargement of an existing line to eight 8 inches or larger over a distance of at least four hundred 400 feet within the corporate city limits of the city of florence as required by the city and paid for by such persons may be recovered by the persons who paid for the same on an equitable prorata basis from water users who subsequently tap such water main as extended or enlarged at right angles to such water main such contracts shall be known as water main rebate agreements b no water main rebate agreement shall be prepared or executed by the city unless such agreement is requested in a written application the form of which shall be provided by the city manager and filed by the person or persons entitled to request such agreement within three 3 months from the date the subject water main extension or enlargement is accepted by the city as determined by the records of the city engineer such date shall be the acceptance date c no water main rebate agreement shall be executed by the city until the city engineer has received and reviewed complete and accurate records and supporting documentation showing the actual cost of the water main extension or enlargement that will be the subject matter of the agreement such records and documentation must be received within six 6 months of the acceptance date any application for a water main rebate agreement which is not supported by such records and supporting documentation shall be an incomplete application an incomplete application shall be void and of no force and effect d no water main rebate agreement shall have a term which ends later than on the fifth anniversary date termination date of the acceptance date provided for in subsection b of this section following the end of such term the city shall have no further obligation and the other party or parties shall have no rights under such agreement other than those accruing prior to the termination date e every water main rebate agreement executed by the city shall be recorded at the expense of the applicant who shall pay such recording costs prior to the recording of the agreement unless recorded no such agreement shall be binding upon the city f no water main rebate agreement shall impose upon the city a duty to collect refund amounts with respect to any new connection to the enlarged or extended water main from the person making such new connection unless the application for the agreement was received by the city prior to the time such new connection was authorized by the city g every water main rebate agreement shall provide that the citys obligations under such agreement shall be limited to the citys using its best efforts to collect prorated refund amounts from those who connect to the extended or enlarged water main after the written application for the agreement has been received by the city and prior to the termination date provided for in the agreement the city may charge the party or parties to the agreement a fee for collecting and distributing said refund amounts h every water main rebate agreement shall also provide that the city shall not be liable to the other party or parties to the agreement for any failure by the city to have collected the appropriate refund amount from a person connecting to the extended or enlarged water main except that the city may be liable with respect to such refund amount if it is proven by clear and convincing evidence in a legal proceeding that such refund was not distributed after collection as a result of fraud i each party to any such agreement must provide to the city prior to preparation and execution of the water main rebate agreement his or her current address and give the city written notice of any change of address occurring during the term of the agreement funds collected by the city pursuant to a water main rebate agreement that are not claimed by the party entitled to receive such funds within one 1 year of the citys sending notice of the receipt of such funds to such party at the last known address of such party shall be forfeited to and become the exclusive property of the city the last known address of any such party shall be the address stated in the agreement or the last address communicated to the city by the written notice of change of address required under this subsection j all calculations of refunds to be collected by the city and distributed to any party or parties under a water main rebate agreement shall be made by the city engineer under the following formula total costs of constructing a line total linear feet of line constructed   total price per foot total price per foot 2   price per foot of frontage total line frontage of property to be served x price per foot of frontage   rebate amount or onehalf of local engineers per foot cost used in estimating x total line frontage of property to be served   rebate amount whichever figure is lower for purposes of the above calculation total cost shall not include equipment depreciation interest on borrowed money or labor overtime calculations of refund amounts shall be based upon the length of frontage of the property of any water user receiving new service from whom rebate amounts are collectable whose property abuts the rightofway or easement containing the extended or enlarged water main k water main rebate agreements are assignable by the developer with the written consent of the city council which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld such assignment shall be in writing and subscribed to by the developer and the city    service outside city water service to customers outside of the city limits is a privilege not a vested right and may be granted terminated or reduced at such time as the city council determines that the supply of treated water is not sufficient to provide such service water service outside the city may in the discretion of the city be conditioned upon an agreement by the owner of said property to consent to or apply for annexation to the city when said property shall be available for annexation part 1990   sale of untreated water the city shall not sell untreated water except for construction use part 1990   regional plant investment fund fees shall be assessed for the regional plant investment fund as agreed by contract between the city of florence town of williamsburg and town of coal creek part 1990   classification of customers for the purpose of this chapter the following classifications are provided a singlefamily dwelling unit a singlefamily dwelling shall be construed as a living unit suitable for occupancy by one 1 or more individuals of a family and forming a separate unit from any other dwelling unit  consisting of one 1 or more habitable rooms arranged occupied or intended or designed to be occupied by not more than one 1 family with facilities for living sleeping cooking and eating b multiplefamily dwellings a multiplefamily dwelling shall consist of a single structure containing more than one singlefamily dwelling unit c hotels and motels a hotel motel or lodge shall be defined as a unit providing overnight sleeping facilities for transient usage d mobile homes mobile homes shall be classified as any unit capable of being transported on wheels behind a standard power unit and which can be moved on normal streets roads and highways said unit must be suitable for living quarters and provide for normal domestic sanitary conveniences e cafes restaurants bars and private clubs cafes restaurants bars and private clubs shall include any establishment providing food or beverage service to the general public or to private membership and where charges for such service of goods and beverages are made such units shall be classified by the square footage therein an area of one thousand 1000 square feet shall be equivalent to a singlefamily dwelling unit f filling stations and garages filling stations and garages shall be defined as service outlets providing for the servicing of motor vehicles monthly fees shall be based on tap size and water usage g commercial laundries public laundries as used herein shall refer to coinoperated laundries and drying facilities for clothing and textile use as well as commercial facilities where such services are provided for the customer on a fee basis monthly fees shall be based on tap size and water usage h schools schools are defined as any private or public institution established and utilized for the instruction of individuals and where said units are to be operational for a period of six 6 months or longer charges shall be based on tap size and water usage i hospitals hospitals shall be defined as either private or public institutions with overnight facilities provided for care of patients charges shall be based on tap size and water usage j other industrial and commercial uses all other commercial and industrial users shall be charged based on tap size water usage and any other criteria set forth in the ordinances lpart 1990   change in customers equipment or service no change in the customers equipment or service shall be made without prior written approval by the city any change in a customers equipment or service which in the city managers evaluation significantly increases the water flow requirement or total quantity of water required by the customer shall require a redetermination of the tap fee and monthly service charge and the customer shall then be responsible for payment of any additional tap fee and service charge so determined the redetermined tap fee shall allow a credit for previously paid tap fees changes in a customers equipment or service which results in a decrease in the service provided by the city shall not however result in a reduction or refund of tap fees part 1990   excessive customer demand any use which requires twenty thousand 20000 gallons of water during a twentyfour 24 hour period must be authorized by the city manager the city manager may impose requirements as to the time of day of the water usage and any other requirement deemed necessary by the city manager to provide water service to all customers part 1990   nonliability of city the city shall not be responsible to the water user for any breakage or defect of service pipes or cocks or any damage caused thereby nor for any failure in the water supply part 1990   water shortages at any time when in the judgment of the city council a shortage of water as supplied by the city waterworks of the city of florence shall seem imminent or likely the city council shall by resolution provide rules and regulations restricting the quantity of water to be used and the hours and manner of its use under emergency circumstances the city manager may impose temporary restrictions part 1990   meter test when the owner of any premises complains of a defective meter the city manager or his assignee upon request may machine test the meter a meter shall be deemed to be working properly when it measures with a range of plus or minus two percent 2% of actual usage if the machine test shows the meter to be working properly a service charge of ten dollars $1000 shall be assessed for all yoketype meter assemblies and meters situated in the basement of buildings and homes where the meter must be dug up to be tested the charge for testing shall be twenty dollars $2000 and the meter reading shall be used to compute excess water charges if the tested meter is in excess of plus or minus two percent 2% of actual usage the water meter shall be replaced and a credit to the customers account computed on the test results shall be given for a three 3month period prior to the testing a travel charge shall be levied for work that is performed at the customers request lpart 1990   city to tap and inspect water mains and equipment in all cases the city or its designee shall make the physical connection of the tap to the water main and shall provide the material and equipment from the water main to the meter setting and shall at all times have the right to inspect the same a curbstop valve shall be located at or near the customers property line all of these services and materials shall be at the owners expense lpart 1990   master meter stationtaps on regional water system a metered water tap with the size determined by the city manager shall be utilized when connections are made to the florence water system under the following circumstances a the connection or service is outside of the florence city limits  b the developer or political entity does not have another water main supply  c the master meter station and tap including but not limited to crossconnection pressure reduction or check valve protection devices are needed to protect the equipment and water quality of the florence water system  d an application for a master meter station has been made to the city of florence administration reviewed by the regional water advisory committee and approved by the florence city council part 1990   tapsmeters each singlefamily dwelling and each unit of a twofamily dwelling shall be required to have a separate tap and shall have a separate meter each individual structure such as a hotel motel or rooming house shall be required to have a separate tap and shall have a separate meter each business or commercial unit shall be required to have a separate tap and shall have a separate meter apartments owned by one 1 owner are not required to have separate meters unless converted to units of separate ownership including but not limited to townhomes and condominiums where two 2 or more dwelling or business units are being served by a single meter each user shall pay the minimum applicable monthly charge as set by resolution and the record owner of the property shall pay all charges for excess water lpart 1990   branching main line meters a installation of main line metering devices shall be required at the expense of the subdivider contractor or customers being served by the branching main line if any of the following circumstances are present 1 the branching main line serves an area that is not to be looped back to the central distribution grid at the time of installation regardless of future plans to do so  2 the water entering the branching main line is to be sold or billed by another entity  3 the branching main line is to enter an area such as an industrial complex multipleuse area or other grounds where numerous taps are to be utilized even if each tap has a separate metering device  4 the branching main lines are eight 8 inches in diameter or larger b branching main line meters are to be used to determine billing accuracy of service line meters leak detection and future consumption planning metering devices are to be sized and rated so as to provide for fire flow and be capable of being serviced and tested without disrupting normal service c in the event a developer who has paid the requisite fee for a tap connection to a branching main line andor installed a branching main line meter to serve a parcel of land changes the development plan to include individual lots with service line tap connections the city council may at its sole discretion allow the developer a credit against the amount paid for the branching main line tap connection for the cost of individual lot service line tap connections at the then current rates under the following circumstances 1 individual lot service line tap connections must be applied for and installed by developer within one 1 year of the date of approval of the final plat pursuant to the florence subdivision regulations unless a further period of time is granted at the discretion of the city council 2 developer must agree to abandon the branch main line tap connection and forfeit any right to the branching main line meter and appurtenances in favor of the city the same to become the sole property of the city  3 said credit applies only to service line tap connections serving individual lots created from land that was the subject of the original proposed development  and 4 developer enters into a written agreement with the city for the credit as herein provided said agreement to be ratified by resolution of the city council  2008   2006  part 1990   special devices required a the city manager or his designee shall determine whether a customer must have a pressure regulating valve and a backflow prevention device and also determine the type and specifications of any necessary device to be installed the customer shall pay for the required material devices and installation of the required pressure regulating valve and backflow prevention device if such installation is not completed within thirty 30 days of notice to customer of the requirement the city shall make such installation and bill the cost thereof as set forth herein and may disconnect customers water service and file a lien on customers property for nonpayment as permitted by law b all installations not performed by the city are subject to city inspection and approval and must be installed in a location that provides access for maintenance testing and repairs c the owner is required to perform annually or pay the city to perform at least annually all tests as required by law on any backflow prevention device installed in accordance with this section if the owner undertakes the inspection he or she must submit a copy of the test results to the city yearly part 1990  2162016   access to premises the city manager water superintendent or designee upon showing proper identification shall have access at reasonable hours to any premises where water is used for the purpose of inspection and examination of the water system part 1990   maintenance of water lines and water meters a no alteration or disconnection in or about any conduit service pipe or water cock or any other apparatus connected therewith shall be made by any person without first obtaining written permission of the city manager or his designee b the city manager shall for cause shown have authority to direct that municipal water meters be moved or placed at a location upon or approximate to the boundary line of the owner user or occupant c water service may be interrupted to make repairs or for other necessary purposes part 1990   meter pits meter pits shall be clearly marked at all times customers shall not conceal obstruct or damage the devices therein a fee shall be assessed to move a metering pit or meter location at the request of the customer the customer shall pay a deposit for charges prior to such action the city shall also assess a fee to the customer to move a meter pit when in the opinion of the city manager the present location is resulting in damage to the meter assembly or creating a safety hazard the customer shall then be assessed a fee for moving said meter pit part 1990   water rates the rates and charges to be collected for the allowance and use of water inside or outside of the florence city limits and for other related water service charges shall be determined by resolution approved by the florence city council for such purpose the current application resolution shall be kept and may be inspected at the city clerks office it is the policy of the city that the water rates encompass reasonable and necessary expenses for debt retirement capital and operating costs of the water system including the acquisition of water the treatment and storage of water and the connection with each of said functions part 1990   water billingadjustments and allowances a all users shall pay monthly that amount billed to the user for water consumption and any other fees at the rate then required by resolution duly adopted b a monthly minimum fee shall be paid by each user or equivalent user physically attached to the water system with additional charges as set forth in  if water service is not physically disconnected to the customer the minimum fee shall include fees for debt retirement and the fee set by resolution for an allowance of water 2 if water service has been interrupted by a citycontrolled valve or means but not physically disconnected from the water system the minimum fee shall include fees for debt retirement but not water use 3 the owner can request a voluntary abandonment thereafter if the service is physically disconnected minimum fees are not required such taps shall be declared abandoned and a new tap or physical connection fee shall be required for reconnection to the water system c payment for debt retirement is required for each space in a privately owned mobile home park regardless of whether the space is then occupied by a mobile home if the mobile home space is not occupied by a mobile home the city will not charge a turnon or turnoff fee if water service at the spaces is controlled by the mobile home park for turning on or turning off the water mobile homes not in privately owned parks shall be considered singlefamily residences and billed as a normal water tap lpart 1990   water billingsadjustments for nonuse while physically connected to the system in the event more than one 1 unit is supplied with water by one 1 tap or meter one 1 of the units is not receiving water service and the property owner wants to receive a credit on his water billing to reflect such lack of use then the following procedure shall be followed a at the time a nonuse is to begin the property owner shall advise the city clerk in writing on forms supplied by the city entitled application for declaring a nonuse of water service this application shall grant to the city the right of entry upon the designated premises to determine whether water is being used b the property owner shall pay a fee of ten dollars $1000 together with the application for declaring a nonuse c the city clerk shall advise the city manager of the application and he or she shall cause an investigation to be made to determine whether it is feasible to place a physical impediment to water use in the premises or unit in which the property owner does not intend to use water if it is feasible in the opinion of the city manager to install such an impediment the same shall be done to the specifications required by the city manager at the expense and direction of the property owner  provided however that the reasonable cost shall not exceed fifty dollars $5000 per unit d the city manager shall also cause periodic inspections of the premises or units which are the subject of the application to be made for the purpose of determining whether the premises is not using water services e in the event that there is tampering of the installed physical impediment to water service or in the event inspection reveals that the designated premises or unit is using water service then the application shall be denied the fee forfeited and no credit allowed on the water billing f at the end of each calendar month but during said month a property owner who has previously submitted an application for declaring a nonuse and paid the required fee shall advise the city clerk whether the premises or unit has used water at any time during that entire month if there has been no use of water during the entire month unless otherwise provided herein the city clerk shall then allow the property owner a credit equal to the monthly minimum charge for that same month  provided however that the property owner shall in any event continue to pay the monthly debt retirement fee for any unit capable of receiving water g in the event that a property owner wilfully misrepresents the water use status of a unit or premises that same person shall be deemed guilty of a misdemeanor and subject to a fine of up to three hundred dollars $30000 or imprisonment for up to ninety 90 days or both such fine and imprisonment in addition all credits previously granted to said property owner shall be reassessed h a new application and fee shall be required each time an owner requests a nonuse status at the premises or unit    bulk water charges the rates regulations and charges to be collected for water sold to bulk water haulers shall be determined by resolution approved by the city council such resolution shall be available for inspection at the city clerks office part 1990   excess water billing water above the monthly minimum gallonage allowance as established by resolution shall be billed monthly when the meter reading has been completed such charges shall be set by resolution by the florence city council part 1990   responsibility for charges the owner of property served with city water shall be responsible for payment of charges for water services supplied by the city however payments may be accepted from tenants on such property all unpaid accounts for water and all other service assessments shall constitute a lien against the subject property and in the event of nonpayment shall be certified to the fremont county treasurer for collection in like manner as are general property taxes part 1990   water tap charges and applications a charges for new
